\n        text = text.strip()\n        \n        # Detect and romanize based on script\n        if self.chinese_pattern.search(text):\n            romanized = self.romanize_chinese(text)\n        elif       logger.info(f\"Fetching {url}\")\n            response = self.session.get(url, timeout=10)\n            response.raise_for_status()\n            \n            # Try to detect encoding\n except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Error fetching {url}: {e}\")\n            return None\n    \n    def extract_leadership_data(self, soup: BeautifulSoup, selectors: Dict, base_url: \n                for leader_elem in leaders:\n                    try:\n                        record = self.parse_leader_element(leader_elem, selectors, base_url, source_lang)\n \n        # Add additional URLs if specified\n        if 'additional_urls' in source_config:\n            urls_to_process.extend(source_config['additional_urls'])\n        \n        for url in urls_to_process[:self.config['max_pages_per_source']]:\n            soup = self.scraper.fetch_page(url)\n            if soup:\n                records = self.scraper.extract_leadership_data(\n                    soup, \n                    source_config.get('selectors', {}),\n                    url,\n                    source_config.get('language', 'auto')\n                )\n                \n                # Add organization context\n                for record in records:\n                    record.organization = source_config['name']\n                    record.role_type = source_config.get('type', 'leadership')\n                \n                all_records.extend(records)\n                logger.info(f\"Found {len(records)} leaders from {url}\")\n        \n        return all_records\n    \n    def export_to_json(self, filename: str = None):\n        \"\"\"Export results to JSON\"\"\"\n        if not filename:\n            filename = f\"leadership_research_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.json\"\n        \n        export_data = {\n            'metadata': {\n                'collection_date': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n Leadership Research'\n            },\n            'leadership_data': [asdict(record) for record in self.results]\n        }\n        \n        with open(filename, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n None):\n        \"\"\"Export results to CSV\"\"\"\n        if not filename:\n            filename = f\"leadership_research_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.csv\"\n        \n        if not self.results:\n            logger.warning(\"No data to export\")\n            return\n        \n        with open(filename, 'w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=asdict(self.results[0]).keys())\n            writer.writeheader()\n            for record in self.results:\n                writer.writerow(asdict(record))\n        \n        logger.info(f\"Exported {len(self.results)} records to {filename}\")\n    \n    def generate_kvp_dataset(self, filename: str = None):\n        \"\"\"Generate KVP simulator compatible dataset\"\"\"\n        if not filename:\n            filename = f\"kvp_leadership_dataset_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.json\"\n        \n        kvp_entities = []\n        \n        for record.title,\n                    'organization': record.organization,\n                    'department': record.department,\n                    'role_type': record.role_type,\n              'collection_date': record.collection_date\n                },\n                'relationships': {\n                    'member_of': record.organization,\n                    'department': record.department if record.department else None\n                },\n                'metadata': {\n                    'confidence': record.confidence,\n                    'data_source': 'web_scraping',\n                    'collection_method': 'automated'\n                }\n            }\n            kvp_entities.append(entity)\n        \n        kvp_dataset = {\n add_person_to_simulation(entity)\n```\n\n### Entity Relationship Modeling\n\n```python\n# Example KVP integration for organizational modeling\ndef create_organizational_network(entities):\n    network = {}\n    \n    for entity in entities:\n        person_id = entity['entity_id']\n        organization = entity['attributes']['organization']\n        title = entity['attributes']['title']\n        \n        # Build hierarchical relationships\n        if organization not in network:\n            network[organization] = {'leaders': [], 'structure': {}}\n        \n        network[organization]['leaders'].append({\n            'id': person_id,\n            'name': entity['attributes']['name'],\n            'title': title,\n            'influence_score': entity['metadata']['confidence']\n        })\n    \n    return network\n```\n\n## Language Processing\n\n### Chinese Text Processing\n\n```python\n# Automatic pinyin romanization\nchinese_name = Track coauthor relationships\n                for coauthor in record.academic_profile.coauthors:\n                    coauthor_networks[person_id].add(coauthor)\n        \n        # Create edges for institutional connections\n        for institution, members in institution_networks.items():\n            if len(members) > 1:\n                # _calculate_technical_capability(self, record) -> float:\n        \"\"\"Calculate technical capability based on education and research\"\"\"\n        score = 0.0\n        \n        if def reduce_opacity_through_academic_cross_reference(self, record, enhanced_record) -> OpacityReductionResult:\n        \"\"\"Calculate opacity reduction achieved through academic record.academic_profile.education:\n            base_score += 0.2\n        \n        # Longer tenure suggests stable patterns\n        if record.years_in_position and record.years_in_position > 3:\n            base_score += 0.2\n        \n        # International exposure suggests predictable behavior patterns\n        if record.academic_profile and record.academic_profile.coauthors:\n            base_score += 0.1\n        \n        return min(1.0, base_score)\n    \n    def _calculate_dual_use_potential(self, record) -> float:\n        \"\"\"Calculate potential for dual-use research applications\"\"\"\n        score = 0.0\n        \n        if record.academic_profile:\n            # Check research areas for dual-use potential\n            research_text = ' '.join(record.academic_profile.research_areas).lower()\n            publications_text = ' '.join(record.academic_profile.notable_publications).lower()\n            combined_text = research_text + ' ' + publications_text\n            \n            for category, keywords in self.dual_use_research_keywords.items():\n                for keyword in keywords:\n                    if keyword in combined_text:\n                        # Weight by strategic importance of the research area\n                        category_weights = {\n                            'cryptography': 0.9,\n 'semiconductors': 0.8,\n                            'nuclear_technology': 1.0,\n                            'aerospace': 0.7,\n                            'surveillance_tech': 0.7\n                        }\n                        score += category_weights.get(category, 0.5) * 0.2\n                        break  # Only count once per category\n        \n        return min(1.0, score)\n    \n    def reduce_opacity_through_academic_cross_reference(self, record, enhanced_record) -> OpacityReductionResult:\n        \"\"\"Calculate opacity reduction achieved through academic cross-referencing\"\"\"\n        original_opacity = self.assess_baseline_opacity(record)\n        enhanced_opacity = self.assess_baseline_opacity(enhanced_record)\n        \n opacity_reduction_percentage=reduction_percentage\n        )\n        \n        # Identify key discoveries\n        if enhanced_record.academic_profile:\n            if result.key_discoveries.append(f\"Technical expertise identified: {', '.join(enhanced_record.academic_profile.research_areas[:3])}\")\n            \n            if
